		isEditor: true,
		releaseMode: false,
		cdnRoot: '/data',
		webSocketHost: '',
		useSecureWebSocket: false
	}


	function startEditor() {
		E2.InitialiseEngi(boot.graphUrl)
	}

	$(document).ready(function() {
		E2.models = {
			user: new User({}),
			graph: new Graph({}),
			fileList: new FileList({})
		}


		if (typeof E2.controllers === 'undefined')
			E2.controllers = {}

		E2.controllers.account = new AccountController()

		startEditor()
	});

    <script>
        Handlebars.registerHelper('abbr-count',function abbrCount(val) {
    var count       = parseInt(val, 10);
    var countString = val + '';
    var symbol      = '';

    if (count >= 1000) {
        symbol = 'k+';
        return countString.substring(0, 1) + symbol;
    }

    return countString;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('calendar',function calendar(timestamp) {
	var time = moment.utc(timestamp);
	return '<span class="moment">' + time.format('MMM DD, YYYY') + '</span>';
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('capitalize',function capitalize(word) {
    return word.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + word.slice(1);
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('chr-gt',function chrGt(str, length, options) {
    if (str.length > length) {
        return options.fn(this);
    } else {
        return options.inverse(this);
    }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('chr-lt',function chrLt(str, length, options) {
    if (str.length < length) {
        return options.fn(this);
    } else {
        return options.inverse(this);
    }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('each-key',function eachKey(object) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
    var ret = '';
    for (var key in object) {
        if (object.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
            ret += options.fn({
                key: key,
                value: object[key]
            });
        }
    }
    return ret;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('each-limit',function eachLimit(context, limit) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
    var ret = '';

    if (context && context.length > 0) {
        var max = Math.min(context.length, limit);
        for (var i = 0; i < max; i++) {
            ret += options.fn(context[i]);
        }
    } else {
        ret = options.inverse(this);
    }

    return ret;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('each-reverse',function eachReverse(context) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
    var ret = '';

    if (context && context.length > 0) {
        for (var i = context.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
            ret += options.fn(context[i]);
        }
    } else {
        ret = options.inverse(this);
    }

    return ret;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('either',function either() {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];

    for (var i = 0; i < arguments.length - 1; i++) {
        if (typeof arguments[i] !== 'undefined' && arguments[i]) {
            return options.fn(this);
        }
    }
    return options.inverse(this);
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('encodeURIComponent',function encodeURIComponentHelper(str) {
    return encodeURIComponent(str);
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('eq',function eq(obj1, obj2, options) {
    if (obj1 === obj2) {
        return options.fn(this);
    } else {
        return options.inverse(this);
    }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('firstof',function firstof() {
    // Use everything, but the options object
    var valuesLength = arguments.length - 1;

    for (var i = 0; i < valuesLength; i++) {
        var value = arguments[i];
        if (value) return value;
    }

    return '';
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('if-gt',function ifGt(a, b) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
    if (a > b) { return options.fn(this); }
    else { return options.inverse(this); }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('if-lt',function ifLt(a, b) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
    if (a < b) { return options.fn(this); }
    else { return options.inverse(this); }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('indefinite-article',function indefiniteArticle(str) {
    if (!str || !str.length) return 'a';
    return (['a','e','i','o','u'].indexOf(str.charAt(0).toLowerCase()) === -1) ? 'a' : 'an';
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('input-select',function inputSelect() {
    var name     = arguments[0];
    var options  = arguments[1];
    var value    = arguments.length > 3 ? arguments[2] : null;

    var html = ['<select name="' + name + '">'];
    for (var i = 0; i < options.length; i++) {
        html.push('<option value="' + options[i].value + '"' + (options[i].selected === true || options[i].value === value ? ' selected="selected"' : '') + '>' + options[i].label + '</option>');
    }
    html.push('</select>');
    return html.join('');
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('iter',function iter(context, options) {
    var fn = options.fn, inverse = options.inverse;
    var ret = "";
    
    if (context && context.length > 0) {
        for (var i = 0, j = context.length; i < j; i++) {
            ret = ret + fn(_.extend({}, context[i], { i: i, iPlus1: i + 1 }));
        }
    } else {
        ret = inverse(this);
    }
    return ret;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('join',function join(array, delimiter) {
    return typeof array.join === 'function' ? array.join((typeof delimiter === 'string') ? delimiter : ',') : '';
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('neither',function neither() {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];

    for (var i = 0; i < arguments.length - 1; i++) {
        if (typeof arguments[i] !== 'undefined' && !arguments[i]) {
            return options.fn(this);
        }
    }
    return options.inverse(this);
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('not-eq',function notEqual(obj1, obj2, options) {
    if (obj1 !== obj2) {
        return options.fn(this);
    } else {
        return options.inverse(this);
    }
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('number',function number(value) {
    return value.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ',');
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('pack-it',function packItHelper(context, options) {
    var packingStructure = [];
    
    if (context.length <= 1) {
        return options.fn({ 'content': context[0], 'size': 1 });
    }
    
    if (context && context.length > 2)
        packingStructure = packIt.getStructure(context, 3, 1);
    else
        packingStructure = [1,1];

    var currRowIndex = 1;
    var packed = _.reduce(context, function (memo, content, i) {
        // First pass of memo is the content object and needs to be run through options.fn
        // i is one ahead at this point so to get the correct packing size we subtract by 1
        memo = typeof memo !== 'string' ? options.fn({ 'content': memo, 'size': packingStructure[i - 1] }) : memo;
        
        var size = packingStructure[i];
        var cell = Object.create(null);
        
        cell.content = content;
        cell.size = size;
        
        if (currRowIndex === 1) {
            cell['position-class'] = 'range-start';
        }
        
        if (currRowIndex === size) {
            cell['position-class'] = 'range-end';
        }
        
        if (currRowIndex === size) {
            currRowIndex = 1;
        } else {
            currRowIndex++;
        }
        
        return memo + options.fn(cell);
    });
    
    return packed;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('paragraphify',function paragraphify(str) {
    return '<p>' + str
        .replace(/^\s\s/, '')
        .replace(/\s*\s$/, '')
        .replace(/(\r?\n)+/, '</p><p>') + '</p>';
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('possessive',function possessive(str) {
    return str + (str.charAt(str.length - 1) === 's' ? '\'' : '\'s');
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('repeat',function repeat(n) {
    var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1], ret = '';
    if (typeof n === 'string') n = parseInt(n, 10);
    for (var i = 0; i < n; i++) {
        ret += options.fn(this);
    }
    return ret;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('subtract',function subtract(object, reducer) {
    return object - reducer;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('title-case',function titleCase(str) {
    if (typeof str === 'undefined') return '';

    return str.replace(/\w\S*/g, function(txt){return txt.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + txt.substr(1).toLowerCase();});
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('truncate',function capitalize(str, length, append) {
    str    = str || '';
    length = length || 10;
    append = typeof append === 'undefined' ? '…' : append;

    if (str.length === length) return str;

    return str.substring(0, length).replace(/\s+$|\.+$/, '') + append;
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('urlify',function urlify(string) {
    if (!string) return '';
    return string.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-').replace(/[^a-z0-9\-]/g, '');
});
Handlebars.registerHelper('ifLengthierThan',function (obj, length)
    {
        var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
        if(obj.length > length)
        {
            return options.fn(this);
        } else
        {
            return options.inverse(this);
        }
    });
Handlebars.registerHelper('friendlyURL',function (url) {
		if (!url)
			return url

		url = url.replace(/.*?:\/\//g, "");
		if (url.endsWith('/'))
			url = url.substring(0, url.length-1);
		return url
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('json',function (obj, options) {
        var j = JSON.stringify(obj)
		if (!j)
			return j

		var deletes = options.hash['deleteKeys'] || ''
		if (deletes) {
			deletes.split(',')
				.forEach(function (d) {
					delete j[d.trim()]
				})
		}
		return j.replace(/<\//gm, '<\\\/') // escape html tag closers
    });
Handlebars.registerHelper('formatDate',function (date) {
		var mdate = moment(date)
		var now = moment(Date.now())

		if (!mdate.isValid())
			return date
		
		if (mdate.isSame(now, 'd'))
			return mdate.calendar()

		if (mdate.isSame(now, 'y'))
			return mdate.format('MMM Do h:mm A')
		
		return mdate.format('ll h:mm A')
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('plural',function (count, what, whats) {
        var plural = (typeof whats === 'string') ? whats : what+'s'
        return count + ' ' + (count === 1  ? what : plural)
    });
Handlebars.registerHelper('select',function (value, options)
    {
        return options.fn(this)
            .replace(new RegExp(' value=\"' + value + '\"'),
                '$& selected="selected"')
            .replace(new RegExp('>' + value + '</option>'),
                ' selected="selected"$&');
    });
Handlebars.registerHelper('concat',function () {
		var i
		var ret = []
		var l = arguments.length - 1
		for (i=0; i<l; i++) {
			ret.push(arguments[i])
		}
		return ret.join("")
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('byindex',function () {
		var opts = []
		for (var l=0; l<arguments.length; l++)
			opts.push(arguments[l])

		opts.pop()		// handlebars stuff

		var index = parseInt(0 + opts.shift())

		if (isNaN(index))
			return '?'
		return opts[index]
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('unescape',function (content) {
		return new Handlebars.SafeString(content)
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('equals',function (arg1, arg2) {
		return arg1 === arg2
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('length',function (arg) {

		if (Array.isArray(arg))
			return arg.length
		if (typeof arg === 'object')
			return Object.keys(arg).length
		return (""+arg).length
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('moment',function (date, fmt) {	// use moment.js to format a date
		if (typeof moment !== 'undefined')
			return moment(date).format(fmt)
		// fallback
		return date.toString()
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('have',function (arg) {
		return (arg && typeof arg === 'object') ? (Object.keys(arg).length > 0) : !!arg
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('and',function () {
		var result = true
		return Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 0,-1)
			.reduce(function(arg){return result && helpers.have(arg)})
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('or',function () {
		var result = false
		Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 0,-1)
			.map(function(arg){
				result = result || helpers.have(arg)
			})
		return !!result
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('makePaginationData',function (meta) {	// used by graphList.handlebars
		return UIPagination.fromMeta(meta)
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('_getQuery',function (queryString) {
		var query = {}

		// if running on client, and no queryString, default to the browser
		if ((typeof queryString === 'undefined') && (typeof window !== 'undefined') && (window.location))
			queryString = window.location.search

		if (queryString && queryString.length && queryString[0] === '?')
			queryString = queryString.substring(1)

		// if queryString found
		if (queryString) {
			for (var pair of queryString.split('&')) {
				pair = pair.split('=')
				if (typeof pair[1] === 'string')
					query[pair[0]] = decodeURIComponent(pair[1])
				else
					query[pair[0]] = pair[1]
			}
		}
		else {
			// assume running on backend
			if (Handlebars._request)	// see app.js
				query = _.extend(query, Handlebars._request.query)
		}
		return query
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('replaceQueryParameters',function (opt) {
		var attributes = []

		var queryString = opt.hash['_']
		delete (opt.hash['_'])

		var query
		if ((typeof helpers !== 'undefined') && (helpers._getQuery))
			query = helpers._getQuery(queryString)
		else if (typeof Handlebars !== 'undefined')
			query = Handlebars.helpers._getQuery(queryString)

		if (!query)
			return '??'

		function isEmpty(value) {
			return (value === false) || (value === null) || (typeof value === 'undefined')
		}
		// clean empty variables from existing query
		for (var attributeName in opt.hash) {
			if (opt.hash.hasOwnProperty(attributeName)) {
				value = opt.hash[attributeName]
				if (isEmpty(value))
					delete query[attributeName]
				else
					query[attributeName] = value
			}
		}

		// join things back
		var ret=[], value
		for (var key of Object.keys(query)) {
			value = query[key]
			if (isEmpty(value))
				ret.push(key)
			else
				ret.push(key+'='+encodeURIComponent(query[key]))
		}
		return '?' + ret.join('&')
	});
Handlebars.registerHelper('ifLengthierThan',function (obj, length)
    {
        var options = arguments[arguments.length - 1];
        if(obj.length > length)
        {
            return options.fn(this);
        } else
        {
            return options.inverse(this);
        }
    });
